[12d[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l[13d[?12l[?25h[?25l[14d[?12l[?25h[?25l[15d[?12l[?25h[?25l[16d[?12l[?25h[?25l[17d[?12l[?25h[?25l[18d[?12l[?25h[?25l[19d[?12l[?25h[?25l[20d[?12l[?25h[?25l[21d[?12l[?25h[?25l7[3;22r8[22d[10S[1;24r[12;1H[36m#[13d# By default the server will pretend to allow ASCII mode but in fact ignore

[53d[?25l[50d[?12l[?25h[?25l[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;53r[53;1H[25S[1;55r[28;9H[36m<div [31mclass=[32m"content_section_text"[36m>[29;11H<p>[30;17H[39m(B[mThis is the default welcome page used to test the correct[31;17Hoperation of the Apache2 server after installation on Ubuntu systems.[32;17HIt is based on the equivalent page on Debian, from which the Ubuntu Apache[33;17Hpackaging is derived.[34;17HIf you can read this page, it means that the Apache HTTP server installed at[35;17Hthis site is working properly. You should (B[0;1m[35m<b>[39m(B[mreplace this file(B[0;1m[35m</b>[39m(B[m (located at[36;17H[36m<tt>[39m(B[m/var/www/html/index.html[36m</tt>[39m(B[m) before continuing to operate your HTTP server.[37;11H[36m</p>[40;11H<p>[41;17H[39m(B[mIf you are a normal user of this web site and don't know what this page is[42;17Habout, this probably means that the site is currently unavailable due to[43;17Hmaintenance.[44;17HIf the problem persists, please contact the site's administrator.[45;11H[36m</p>[47;9H</div>[48;9H<div [31mclass=[32m"section_header"[36m>[49;11H<div [31mid=[32m"changes"[36m></div>[50;17H[39m(B[mConfiguration Overview[51;9H[36m</div>[52;9H<div [31mclass=[32m"content_section_text"[36m>
[31d[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l[37d[?12l[?25h[?25l[43d[?12l[?25h[?25l[49d[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;53r[53;1H[25S[1;55r[28;11H[36m<p>[29;17H[39m(B[mUbuntu's Apache2 default configuration is different from the[30;17Hupstream default configuration, and split into several files optimized for[31;17Hinteraction with Ubuntu tools. The configuration system is[32;17H(B[0;1m[35m<b>[39m(B[mfully documented in[33;17H/usr/share/doc/apache2/README.Debian.gz(B[0;1m[35m</b>[39m(B[m. Refer to this for the full[34;17Hdocumentation. Documentation for the web server itself can be[35;17Hfound by accessing the [36m<a [31mhref=[32m"/manual"[36m>[39m(B[mmanual[36m</a>[39m(B[m if the [36m<tt>[39m(B[mapache2-doc[36m</tt>[36;17H[39m(B[mpackage was installed on this server.[38;11H[36m</p>[39;11H<p>[40;17H[39m(B[mThe configuration layout for an Apache2 web server installation on Ubuntu systems is as follows:[41;11H[36m</p>[42;11H<pre>
[43d[39m(B[m/etc/apache2/
[44d|-- apache2.conf
[45d|[9G`--  ports.conf
[46d|-- mods-enabled
[47d|[9G|-- *.load
[48d|[9G`-- *.conf
[49d|-- conf-enabled
[50d|[9G`-- *.conf
[51d|-- sites-enabled
[52d|[9G`-- *.conf
[30d[?12l[?25h[?25l[36d[?12l[?25h[?25l[42d[?12l[?25h[?25l[48d[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;53r[53;1H[25S[1;55r[28;11H[36m</pre>[29;11H<ul>[30;25H<li>[31d<tt>[39m(B[mapache2.conf[36m</tt>[39m(B[m is the main configuration[32;28Hfile. It puts the pieces together by including all remaining configuration[33;28Hfiles when starting up the web server.[34;25H[36m</li>[36;25H<li>[37d<tt>[39m(B[mports.conf[36m</tt>[39m(B[m is always included from the[38;28Hmain configuration file. It is used to determine the listening ports for[39;28Hincoming connections, and this file can be customized anytime.[40;25H[36m</li>[42;25H<li>[43d[39m(B[mConfiguration files in the [36m<tt>[39m(B[mmods-enabled/[36m</tt>[39m(B[m,[44;28H[36m<tt>[39m(B[mconf-enabled/[36m</tt>[39m(B[m and [36m<tt>[39m(B[msites-enabled/[36m</tt>[39m(B[m directories contain[45;28Hparticular configuration snippets which manage modules, global configuration[46;28Hfragments, or virtual host configurations, respectively.[47;25H[36m</li>[49;25H<li>[50d[39m(B[mThey are activated by symlinking available[51;28Hconfiguration files from their respective[52;28H*-available/ counterparts. These should be managed
[29d[?12l[?25h[?25l[35d[?12l[?25h[?25l[41d[?12l[?25h[?25l[47d[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;53r[53;1H[25S[1;55r[28;28Hby using our helpers[29;28H[36m<tt>[30;33H[39m(B[ma2enmod,[31;33Ha2dismod,[32;28H[36m</tt>[33;28H<tt>[34;33H[39m(B[ma2ensite,[35;33Ha2dissite,[36;29H[36m</tt>[37d[39m(B[mand[38;28H[36m<tt>[39;33H[39m(B[ma2enconf,[40;33Ha2disconf[41;28H[36m</tt>[39m(B[m. See their respective man pages for detailed information.[42;25H[36m</li>[44;25H<li>[45d[39m(B[mThe binary is called apache2. Due to the use of[46;28Henvironment variables, in the default configuration, apache2 needs to be[47;28Hstarted/stopped with [36m<tt>[39m(B[m/etc/init.d/apache2[36m</tt>[39m(B[m or [36m<tt>[39m(B[mapache2ctl[36m</tt>[39m(B[m.[48;28H(B[0;1m[35m<b>[39m(B[mCalling [36m<tt>[39m(B[m/usr/bin/apache2[36m</tt>[39m(B[m directly will not work(B[0;1m[35m</b>[39m(B[m with the[49;28Hdefault configuration.[50;25H[36m</li>[51;11H</ul>[52;9H</div>
[28d[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l[34d[?12l[?25h[?25l[40d[?12l[?25h[?25l[46d[?12l[?25h[?25l[52d[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;53r8[53d[25S[1;55r[2;1H[K[29;9H[36m<div [31mclass=[32m"section_header"[36m>[30;13H<div [31mid=[32m"docroot"[36m></div>[31;17H[39m(B[mDocument Roots[32;9H[36m</div>[34;9H<div [31mclass=[32m"content_section_text"[36m>[35;13H<p>[36;17H[39m(B[mBy default, Ubuntu does not allow access through the web browser to[37;17H[36m<em>[39m(B[many[36m</em>[39m(B[m file apart of those located in [36m<tt>[39m(B[m/var/www[36m</tt>[39m(B[m,[38;17H[36m<a [31mhref=[32m"http://httpd.apache.org/docs/2.4/mod/mod_userdir.html"[36m [31mrel=[32m"nofollow"[36m>[39m(B[mpublic_html[36m</a>[39;17H[39m(B[mdirectories (when enabled) and [36m<tt>[39m(B[m/usr/share[36m</tt>[39m(B[m (for web[40;17Happlications). If your site is using a web document root[41;17Hlocated elsewhere (such as in [36m<tt>[39m(B[m/srv[36m</tt>[39m(B[m) you may need to whitelist your[42;17Hdocument root directory in [36m<tt>[39m(B[m/etc/apache2/apache2.conf[36m</tt>[39m(B[m.[43;13H[36m</p>[44;13H<p>[45;17H[39m(B[mThe default Ubuntu document root is [36m<tt>[39m(B[m/var/www/html[36m</tt>[39m(B[m. You[46;17Hcan make your own virtual hosts under /var/www. This is different[47;17Hto previous releases which provides better security out of the box.[48;13H[36m</p>[49;9H</div>[51;9H<div [31mclass=[32m"section_header"[36m>[52;11H<div [31mid=[32m"bugs"[36m></div>
[33d[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l[39d[?12l[?25h[?25l[45d[?12l[?25h[?25l[51d[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;53r[53;1H[25S[1;55r[28;17HReporting Problems[29;9H[36m</div>[30;9H<div [31mclass=[32m"content_section_text"[36m>[31;11H<p>[32;17H[39m(B[mPlease use the [36m<tt>[39m(B[mubuntu-bug[36m</tt>[39m(B[m tool to report bugs in the[33;17HApache2 package with Ubuntu. However, check <a[34;17H[31mhref=[32m"https://bugs.launchpad.net/ubuntu/+source/apache2"[35;17H[31mrel=[32m"nofollow"[39m(B[m>existing bug reports[36m</a>[39m(B[m before reporting a new bug.[36;11H[36m</p>[37;11H<p>[38;17H[39m(B[mPlease report bugs specific to modules (such as PHP and others)[39;17Hto respective packages, not to the web server itself.[40;11H[36m</p>[41;9H</div>[46;7H</div>[47;5H</div>[48;5H<div [31mclass=[32m"validator"[36m>[49;5H</div>[50;3H</body>
[51d</html>
